 ACHARNENSES 19

 explicat W. G. Clark, “Before a foreign vessel was allowed to
 unload her cargo or even moor alongside the quay, a custom-
 house ofﬁcer went out in a boat (ἐκπλεύσας σκάφει) and examined
 the cargo to ascertain the amount of duty payable by the
 owner. If he found among the cargo any article not included in
 the bill of lading, he had the right to denounce it as contraband,
 to seize and sell it. If be exceeded his powers, the injured
 owner would appeal to his country for redress.”
